 The state government fears that private milk unions are making 5 times the profits, putting a burden on the consumer's pockets

 He said that Mishra's allegations for the anti-corruption movement are extremely harsh
 kumaar ke mutabik wo arvind kejariwal ko pichley 12 saalon se jaanate hai auravo kabhi bhrasht nahin ho sakate
 Kumar Vishwas believes that even Kejriwal's enemies cannot accuse him of such
 unhone in aaropon par sabooton kii bhi maang kii
 Vishwas said that if Kapil Mishra really had such information, then he should have put it on the platform of Yebat party
 'ekala chalo re'kumaar vishwaas ke twit ko retweet karte hue kapil mishra ne likhaa, 'jis din satyendra jain jail jaaenge, us din to aap bhi maanoge bhaiya
 Till then “ekla Chalo Re
 "jis din satyendra jain jail jaaenge, us din to aap bhi maanoge bhaiya
 Until then "ekla Chalo Re" https: / / t
 co / uszcmk4fpc— Kapil Mishra (@kapilmishraaap)may 7, 2017yogendra yadav ne bhi kiya bachaavam aadmi party ke purv netaa yogendra yadav ne kapil mishra par hi sawaal uthaae hai
 Yogendra Yadav clearly stated that Kejriwal can never take a bribe
 unhone kaha ki itane gambhir aarope aise halke dhang se nahin lagane chahie
 He also said why Kapil Mishra was sitting still till now
 vahiin duusari taraf aam aadmi party ke varisht netasanjay sinhane bhi kejariwal ke samarthan main khadey najar aae
 Sanjay wrote in his tweet, 'arvind Kejriwal's honesty is not doubted even by his enemy, Kapil Mishra's statement that he was in a dilemma to go for the post of minister is lousy and cheap
 'bataa den ki ravivaar subah purv mantri kapil mishra ne kejariwal par dilli ke mantri satyendra jain se do karod rupee lene kaa aarope lagaaya tha
 Kapil said that he saw Kejriwal taking money in front of his eyes on Friday
 desh main aam chunaav kaa mausam aane se pehle centre or rajya sarkaron ne ek phir kisaanon kii sud lenaa shuru kar diya he
 First, the Center announced a major relief for the sugarcane farmers to pay their dues, while now Bihar has started the state 'crop Assistance Scheme' for the benefit of farmers suffering from the weather
 mukhyamantri nitish kumaar kii mahatvakankshi rajya'fasal sahaayta yojana'se mausam kii maar kii vajah se fasal nuksaan kaa saamana karne vaale bihar ke lakhon kisaanon ko phayda milegaa
 Earlier, the Pradhan Mantri Fasal Bima Yojana was running in the state, but farmers did not get much compensation in it
 rajya sarkaar nekisanonke liye 'samaveshi fasal sahaayta yojana' ke naam se ek vishesh fasal beemaa yojana bhi shuru kii he
 After the implementation of this scheme, whatever new crop insurance schemes were already running in the state, this new scheme has been replaced
 haal main hueupachunaavamein haar ke baad apana janaadhar bachaae rakhane kii koshishon main juty nitish sarkaar kii ore se ise bada daanv mana ja rahaa he
 At the same time, the Center has also given its approval to the plan to provide bailout package of Rs 8,500 crore for sugarcane farmers
 kitna milegaa phayda'fasal sahaayta yojana' ke tahat bihar ke kisaanon ko unke fasal kharaab hone kii sthiti par rajya sarkaar muaavja degi
 To take advantage of the scheme, farmers have to register on the online portal every Kharif and Rabi crop season
 yojana ke tahat fasal kii vaastavik upaj dar main 20% tak kii kami hone par 7,500 rupee prati hectare kii dar se adhiktam 15 hajaar or 20% se adhik kshati par 10 hajaar rupee prati hectare kii dar adhiktam 20 hajaar rupee die jaaenge
 Both the raiyat or non-raiyat farmers can avail this scheme
 laabh lene ke liye raiyat kisaanon ko apni jameen kaa kaagaj prastut karnaa hoga, jabaki gaiyr raiyat kisaanon ko ek swa-ghoshnaptr dena hoga, jo kisaan salaahkaar yaa ward sadsy se sweekrut hoga
 Out of Bihar PM Crop Insurance Scheme, the scheme was approved during a cabinet meeting chaired by Chief Minister Nitish Kumar at his official residence
 iske saath hi bihar pradhanmantri fasal beemaa yojana ke daayre se nikalne vaala desh kaa pehla rajya ban gaya he
 Earlier, under the Prime Minister's Crop Insurance Scheme, the Center had to pay 49 percent, the state 49 percent and the farmer 2 percent as part of the premium amount, but only a few indebted farmers could get the benefit
 rajya kii sahakaarita vibhaag ke pradhan sachiv atul prasad ne bataaya ki varsh 2016 ke aankadon ke mutabik pradhanmantri fasal beemaa yojana ke tahat rajya sarkaar kii premium raashi 495 karod thi jabaki kisaanon ko milane vaali raahat raashi maatr 221 karod rahi
 For this reason, this new inclusive 'bihar State Crop Assistance Scheme' has been launched to provide relief to all sections of the farmers of the state
 is yojana kii shuruyaat karne ke saath hi bihar aisa pehla rajya ban gaya he jahaan kisaanon ko fasal nuksaan par raahat dene ke liye is prakaar kii yojana kii shuruyaat kii gai he
 After the implementation of this new scheme of the state government, the Pradhan Mantri Crop Insurance Scheme and any other type of insurance scheme will now be closed to benefit the farmers in the state
 ikkisvin sadi kaa itihaas likhte hue yah jarur darj hoga ki china shaayad utani teji se nahin badla jitani teji se uske bare main duniya kaa najariya badla
 It was this September when almost all the global heads of state including the Indian Prime Minister were present in the US but the eyes of importance were only on the visit of Chinese President Xi Jinping to America, who reached Beijing to ensure that China's currency was yuan ( (also known as renminbi) will be included in the elite club of currency which has so far only US dollars, Japanese Ukraine, has replaced the British pound and euro
 sitambar main washington ke kootnithik galiyaaron main tairti rahi yah muhim, beete pakhwaade badi khabar bani jab iemef ne elaan kiya ki uske visheshgy esadiar main yuan ke pravesh par raji hai
 With this, it was decided that in October 2016, the formalities of making the Yuan the fifth most powerful currency in the world will be completed
 esadiar main yuan ke pravesh se duniya kii duusari sabase badi arthvyavastha ke liye aisi saakh mili he jiskaa koi sani nahin he
 For countries caught in the foreign exchange crisis, the support of IMF is the last resort which was recently given to Greece or other crisis countries of Europe and India in 1991
 iemef ke tahat esadiar yani special drawing ritis ek sankatkalin vyavastha he
 SDR is a type of currency that is counted as part of the IMF member countries' foreign exchange reserves
 sankat ke samay iske badale iemef se sansaadhan milte hai
 SDR is a technical arrangement that is unfortunately needed but indirectly the club is the basis for the formation of the world's foreign exchange reserves
 duniya ke lagbhag sabhi deshon ke videshi mudra bhandar dollar, yen, pound or euro par aadhaarit hai, yuan ab inamen paanchavin karency hogi
 SDR has made very few headlines in its 46-year history
 is darje ko paane ke liye iemef kii sharten itani kathin hai ki koi desh is taraf dekhtaa hi nahin
 The euro formed part of it in 2001 by the merger of several European currencies
 kisi mudra ke liye iemef ke moolyankan kii do sharten hai
 The first condition is that the country issuing this currency should be a big exporter
 vishwa niryaat main 11 fisadi hisse ke saath china is paimaane par badi takat he
 On the scale of exports, the yuan ranks third after the dollar and euro, with the yen and pound lagging far behind
 esadiar club main sadsyta kii duusari shart he ki karency kaa mukt rup se istemaal ho sake
 China probably does not live up to this scale, because the yuan is banned and its price is not even the market, but the government decides, but it is China's opinion that the IMF has changed the definition for the yuan on the scale of free currency
 iemef kaa tark he ki antarrashtriya vinimay main yuan kaa hissaa kaaphi bada he
 In 2014 it was the seventh largest currency in the currency reserves of various countries
 global karency spot trading main yuan 11veen or bond bazaaron main saatvin sabase badi karency he
 This was the reason that despite being irreversible, Yuan got a status that is almost impossible
 yuan kii yah oonchai, bade badlaav lekar aegi
 With the introduction of the fifth currency in the SDR, the countries of the world will reorganize their foreign exchange reserves and increase the share of the yuan in the next few months
 mana ja rahaa he ki kareeb ek trillian dollar ke antarrashtriya videshi mudra bhandar yuan main badale jaaenge yani ki dollar kii tarj par yuan kii maang bhi badhegi
 The World Bank believes that over the next five years the world's companies will issue large-scale yuan-centric bonds, which the financial market calls 'panda Bonds'
 inkaa aakaar 50 arab dollar tak ja saktaa he jo vittiya bazaaron main isaki hanak kai guna badhayega
 The yuan has moved towards making itself a global reserve currency
 global bazaaron main british pound kaa asar simit he, japani yen ek dhahati hui karency he or euro kaa bhavishya asthir he
 Therefore, the US dollar and yuan will probably be the two most prominent currencies in the world
 darasal, china chahta bhi yahi tha, isliye yuan kaa esadiar main aana keval ek vittiya ghatana nahin he balki isse global aarthik-rajnatik santulan main ve badlaav shuru honge jinka akalan varshon se ho rahaa tha
 In fact, from here the debate on the dollar monopoly countdown in the world is starting with more fact and shock, because about 45 percent of the world's inland exchanges are in US dollars, which requires the US banking system, soon
 Yuan will get a large part of it
 china jis global aarthik takat banane ke safar par he, usamen yuan kaa yah darja sabase ahm padaav he, lekin isse zyada mahatvapurn yah he ki darasal china utana nahin badla he jitna ki duniya kaa najariya china ke prati badal gaya he
 There is no democracy in China even today and the financial system is as opaque as before, again the world has accepted the power of China
